# mindscapes
REPO for Mindscape Project

Members: Rita Borgo, Maria Teresa Ortoleva, Karolina Szafranek

###Needed:
MongoDB and Node.js
###To run application:

**Connect to MongoDB**
```
cd server
mongod --config /usr/local/etc/mongod.conf --fork
```
And populate with test data
```
use mindscapes

```

**Run back-end server**

(in a new terminal window)
```
npm start
```

**Run react client:**

(in yet another terminal window)
```
cd ..
cd mindscapes-app
npm start
```
